0b1(mani bka' 'bum): rga ga ra skad du
1a1(mani bka' 'bum): chos skyong ba'i rgyal po bsrong btsan rgam po'i bka' 'bum las bstod kyi cha thog mar bla ma rgyud pa'i gsol 'debs lo rgyus sogs bzhugs spyon
1b1(mani bka' 'bum): oM ma NAM pad maud+d+ho/ rang bzhin gdod nas dag pa'i chos nyid la// smyos pa'i mdzan mA k+Shan g+hAm+b+ha rab dben zhing // mnyam nyod myig yo rgyal ba kun gyi thugs// chom/ 
1b2(mani bka' 'bum): sku 'od dpag med la phyag 'tshal lo// skye med rnam par dag pa'i dbyings nyid las// ma 'gags ye shes chen po'i rgyal gyis ni// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor rang gos la kun la khyab// longs
1b3(mani bka' 'bum): sku spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// zung 'jug dag pa'i mkha' klong yangs pa las// thugs rje chen po'i nyi 'od rab gsal zhing // 'gro kun ma rig mun pa sel mdzad pa'i// chos
1b4(mani bka' 'bum): rgyu lo sprul pa'i sku la phyag 'tshal lo// rgyal ba kun gyi sras mchog rdo rje'i sku// ston pa'i rgyal tshab 'gro ba'i dpal mgon du// sangs rgyas kun gyis dbang bskur rjes gnang ba// u rgyan pad
1b5(mani bka' 'bum): me'i sku la phyag 'tshal lo// rgyal dang de sras rnams kyis lung bstan zhing // gsang gter kun gyi bdag nyid brtul shugs spyod// thegs pa mchog gis 'gro rnams smin mdzad pa'i// grub thob/ 
1b6(mani bka' 'bum): dngos grub zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// mkhyen pa'i mnga' bdag 'jam dpal gzhon nu'i sku// kha ba can du bstan pa rgyas mdzad pa'i// chos kyi rgyal po khri bsrong lde btsan gyi// sprul pa
1b7(mani bka' 'bum): mnga' bdag nyang la phyog 'tshal lo// rigs ldan gong ma'i sras su sku 'khrungs shing // mkhyen rtogs ljon shing rnam grol 'bras bus mdzes// 'gro ba'i mi shes rgud pa sal mdzad pa'i// 
2a1(mani bka' 'bum): da na na / rnam ma nan rna na nagan tu madran rban ba rnam mang // 'ad dang du ldam sa rgyags na ma mdza pa
2a2(mani bka' 'bum): bzang po'i mtshan can de la phyag 'tshal lo// spyan ras gzigs sgyul rgyal bas lung bstan zhing // bstan pa'i zhabs tog 'gro kun dang ba 'dren// thugs rje'i stobs kyis 'gro don dpag med
2a3(mani bka' 'bum): mdzad/ lha rje dge ba 'bu mo la phyag 'tshal lo// sgrol mas byin brlabs rang bzhin rnal 'byor ma// ye shes sgyu ma'i lus kyis 'gro ba kun// rtsod bral dag pa'i lam la 'god mdzad pa'i// 
2a4(mani bka' 'bum): mo ye shes mchog la phyag 'tshal lo// 'jig rten 'di yi zhon 'dzin kun dor nas// 'jig rten phyi ma'i gtan gyi bde ba tshil// gcig pur dka' ba spyod pa'i mthu stobs can// byang sems
2a5(mani bka' 'bum): chu sgom pa la phyag 'tshal lo// mkhas grub dam pa mang po mnyes byas nas// zab lam snyan rgyu de rtogs pa'i gter mdzod brnyes// rgya gar lan gsum bgrod pa'i brtul shugs can// mthu/ 
2a6(mani bka' 'bum): bzhi bya bral ba la phyag 'tshal lo// thos bsam lung rigs tshogs la ma rmongs shing // 'chad rtsod brtsam pa'i tshul la blo gros rgyas// bshad grub gnyis kyis sangs rgyas bstan pa 'dzin
2a7(mani bka' 'bum): bsod nams seng ge'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// smon lam rnam dag rigs kyi rgyud par 'gyur// dgongs pa rnam dag byang chub sems gnyis sbyang // phrin las rnam dag rgyal ba'i zhabs/ 
2b1(mani bka' 'bum): tog bsgrub// bkra shis rgyal mtshan zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// gzhon nu'i'o dus nas theg chen chos dang phrad// zhabs tog gsum gyis bla ma mnyes par mdzad// khyad par man ngag 'di'i mdzod 'dzin/ 
2b2(mani bka' 'bum): pa/ blo gros rgyal mtshan zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// gangs can 'phags pa'i bstan pa rin po che// mi nub phyogs bcur dar zhing rgyas par mdzad// byams dang thugs rjes 'gro rnams grol mdzad
2b3(mani bka' 'bum): pa'i/ 'phags mchog ner bzang dpal la phyag 'tshal lo// srid pa'i bde 'byor rmi lam ltar rtogs nas// sbas pa'i tshul 'dzin rtse gcig sgrub la brtson// byang chub thugs gnyis 'byongs pa'i rin
2b4(mani bka' 'bum): po che/ bzang po rgyal mtshan zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// dpal ldan sangs rgyas bstan pa 'dzin pa la// dpal ldan sangs rgyas mkhas pa'i dbang po mchog/ dpal ldan sangs rgyas shin du chos
2b5(mani bka' 'bum): kyi rje dpal ldan sangs rgyas zhabs lo phyag 'tshal lo// bsam yas bsam gyis mi khyab rgyal ba'i gnas// grub kyang grub pa'i dbang phyug tha mal tshul// dpal mgon dpal ldan bla ma'i mtshan
2b6(mani bka' 'bum): nyid kun/ yongs rdzogs yongs 'dzin mchog la phyag 'tshal lo// lung gi dam chos legs par 'chad la mkhas// rdzogs pa'i dam chos legs par sgrub lnga brtson// rgyal ba'i dam chos rnyeg
2b7(mani bka' 'bum): bar 'dzin pa'i mchig/ 'dren mchog chos legs zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// 'gro drug kun la thugs rje'i spyan gyis gzigs// stong nyid thugs rje dbyer med thugs mnga' bas// 'gro ba
3a1(mani bka' 'bum): sdug bsngal thams cad spel mdzad pa'i// thugs rje chen po nyid la phyag 'tshal lo// lus can kun gyi phan bde sgrub pa'i phyir// rgyal ba kun gyis mkhyen brtse gcog bsdus nas// phrin las/ 
3a2(mani bka' 'bum): rnam bzhi thogs med sgrub mdzad ma// ye shes mkha' 'gro'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal lo// bskal pa'i me ltar 'bar ba'i klong dkyil nas// rgyal ba'i bka' bzhin bstan pa bsrung mdzad pa// zhing bcu
3a3(mani bka' 'bum): sgrol mdzad drag po'i 'khor dang bcas// chos skyong bsrungs ma'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo// rgyud pa'i bla ma rnams la gsol gtab pas// bdag dang na mkha' mnyam pa'i sems can rnams// 
3a4(mani bka' 'bum): bde ba can gyi zhing mchog dram pa der// rdzus skyes 'od dpag med kyi zhal mthong shog/ skye zhing skye ba dag ni thams cad du// rigs bzang blo gsal nga rgyal med pa dang // snying rje che zhing bla ma la
3a5(mani bka' 'bum): gus ldan// spyan ras gzigs kyi dam tshig la gnas shog// oM ma Ni pad me hUM/ chos dbyings spros bral rgyal ba 'od dpag med// bde chen longs sku
3a6(mani bka' 'bum): mgon po spyan ras gzigs// sbrul sgra 'gro ba'i don mdzad bsrung btsan rgam// zlum dag gzung 'jug gsum la gsil ba 'debs// 'gyur med rdo rje'i sku mchog pad ma 'byung // gas
3a7(mani bka' 'bum): sngags brtul shugs spyod pa'i dngos grub nabs// mkhyen brtse nus par ldan pa'i mnga' bdag nying // theg mchog bdag po gsum la gsol ba 'debs// rims sogs yon tan kun
3b1(mani bka' 'bum): ldan mi bskyod pa// thabs mkhas thugs rje ldan pa'i shAkya bzang // 'gro ba'i nad gso mdzad pa'i dge ba 'bum// phrin las mthar byin gsum la gsol ba 'debs// lam mchog grub pa brnyes pa'i ye shes/ 
3b2(mani bka' 'bum): mchog tu dka' spyad mtha' ru phyin pa'i chu sgom pa// chos brgyad 'khrul pa zhig pa'i mtha' zhi pa// skyes bu dam pa gsum la gsol ba 'debs// ru bzhi mkhas pa'i dbang po bsod nams seng // lhag pA/ 
3b3(mani bka' 'bum): lha yis rjes bzung bkra shis rgyal// dam pas byin brlabs drin can sku 'bum pa// thar pa'i lam ston gsum la gsol ba 'debs// 'jig rten kun las 'phags pa'i nor bzang dpal// tshe 'di blos
3b4(mani bka' 'bum): gtang bzeng bzang po rgyal mtshan zhabs// mkhas pa'i gtsug brgyan mkhas grub chos kyi rje// thar pa'i ded dpon gsum la gsol ba 'debs// bslab gsuM rnam par dag pa'i bsam grub dpal// lung rtog
3b5(mani bka' 'bum): mnga' bdag chos legs mtshan can zhabs// rtsa ba rgyud pa'i bla ma khyed rnams la// rab gus gdung ba drag pos gsol ba 'debs// rgyud pa kun 'dus rtsa ba'i bla ma dang // dngos grub kun rtsi la yi dam lha tshogs
3b6(mani bka' 'bum): dang / bar chad kun sel mkha' 'gro chos skyong ste// yid bzhin nor bu gsum la gsol ba 'debs// dngos rgyud bla ma rnams la gsol btab pas// ma dag snod kyi 'jig rten 'di nyid ni// rin chen sna
3b7(mani bka' 'bum): tshogs las gru'i dag pa'i zhing // bde brtson du 'gyur bar byin gyis brlabs// dngos rgyud bla ma rnams la gsom btab pas// tha ma la lus kyi zhen pa kun dril nas// sdang la rang bzhin med pa lnga masku
4a1(mani bka' 'bum): thugs rje chen po'i sku ru byin gyis brlobs// dngos rgyud bla ma rnams la gsol btab pas// tha mal ngag gi zhen pa kun byal nas// grag stong 'gag pa med pa lnga yi sku// thugs rje
4a2(mani bka' 'bum): chen po'i gsung du byin gyis brlobs// dngos rgyud bla ma rnams la gsol btab pas// tha mal yid kyi zhen pa kun bral nas// gsal snying mtha' bral na mkha' lta bu'i dbyings// thugs rje chen po
4a3(mani bka' 'bum): thugs su byin gyis brlobs// khyer so gsum gyi rnal 'byor nyams blangs pas// mi 'gyur rdo rje gsum la gnas pa yis// snyig mA sgo gsum sgrib pa kun sbyangs nas// dag pa'i sku gsung thugs
4a4(mani bka' 'bum): su byin gyis brlabs// / nye brgyud ni// // oM ma Ni pad me hUM/ mi dbang thugs rje'i mnga' bdag bsrong btsan rgom// de yi rnam sprul gter gton shAkya bzang / 
4a5(mani bka' 'bum): chos rgyal gnyis pa lha rje dge ba 'bum// sprul pa'i sku mchog gsum la gsol ba 'debs// oM ma Ni pad me hUM/ 'phags ma sgrol mas byin brlabs ye shes mchog/ mkhas shing grub pa brnyes/ 
4a6(mani bka' 'bum): pa'i dngos grub bzang // ma nor lam ston blo gros rin chen zhabs// skyes bu dam pa gsum la gsol ba 'debs// mkhyen rtogs nus pa phul phyin shes rab dpal// lung dang rtogs pa'i mdzad 'dzin shes
4a7(mani bka' 'bum): rab 'od/ yi dam lha yi rjes bzung bkra shis rgyal// nal 'byor dbang phyug gsum la gso 'debs// / dge 'bum rnam 'phrul blo gros rgyal mtshan zhabs// rgyal ba'i sras po 'phags mchog nor bu na
4b1(mani bka' 'bum): 'jig rten chos brgyad spangs pa'i bzang rgyal ba// bya btang chen po gsum la gsol ba 'debs// mkhas grub chen po dpal gyi mtshan can zhabs// mkhas btsun grub pa brnyes pa'i bsam grub dpal// yongs
4b2(mani bka' 'bum): rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag chos legs zhabs// bstan pa'i gsal byed gsum la gsol ba 'debs// rgyud pa kun 'dus rtsa ba'i bla ma dang // zhes sogs gong ltar bya'o// / 
4b3(mani bka' 'bum): ga ci ga ba kya / ga zugs// / oM me Ni pad me hUM/ thugs rje'i bdag po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo// nub phyogs bde ba can gyi zhing lam
4b4(mani bka' 'bum): nas/ sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas 'od dpag med kyi sprul pa/ byang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis 'gro ba sems can gyi don gyis gcig par lung thob nas/ 'gro drug gi sems can
4b5(mani bka' 'bum): la thugs rje'i spyan gyis rgyun chad med par gzigs pa yin no// de nas bskrun pa'i bdag po sangs rgyas shAkya thub pas/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis byang phyogs kha ba can gyi rgyal khams dus sdigs/ 
4b6(mani bka' 'bum): ma lnga brgya la 'dul bar gzigs nas lung bstan no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' des dus kyi skyegs ma lnga la 'dul ba'i dus la khyab par gzigs nas/ bad blo bur gyi rgyal po bslong btson nam por sprul nas/ 
4b7(mani bka' 'bum): rus 'phrul sdang dang / mtha' 'dul dang / yang 'dul dang / ru gno bzhi la sogs pa'i gtsug lago khang brgyam brgyad bo zhings/ rin po che dang / khrem bu zhog pa dang / brag lha mgon po rnams btsun mo rnams kyis
5a1(mani bka' 'bum): bzhengs so// rgya gar gyi slob dpon d+harma ko sha dang / rgya nag gi slob dpon ta shang mahA ya na dang / lo tsA wa thon mi sam b+ho tra dang / lha lung rdo rje dpal dang / a tsar+ya a lo ka dang / lang 'gro ye shes dpal/ 
5a2(mani bka' 'bum): dang / lo paN mang pos chos bka' mdo sde mang po bsgyur ro// khyad par du thugs rje chen po'i mang rgyud nyi shu rtsa gtsug bsgyur ro// de'i nang nas kyang yig drug pa bsgyur ro// de la chos skyong ba'i rgyal po chen po/ 
5a3(mani bka' 'bum): glegs bam ngal mtshar/ le'u zhe gcig ces 'byung yang / dkyus na la'u ma drugs mi med pas de byang bar byar// thugs rje chen po'i sbrul pa des/ thugs rje chen po'i yig drug pa 'di la bskor gsum du mdzad to// mdo bskor dang / smra/ 
5a4(mani bka' 'bum): bskor dang / zhal gdams kyi bskor dang gsum/ de la mdo bskor la/ lo rgyus chen mo le'u sum bcu rtsa drug pa/ za ma tog gi mdo dang / phyag stong spyan stong gi gzungs dang gsum mo// / gter gyi la byang nags
5a5(mani bka' 'bum): kha me 'dug kyang / mad bskor gyi la chan la the zhing / tshas rgyas bsrong bcar nas po bka' yin ngas la me tog rgyan par ning bkod/ bka' chems 'thon 'bring ma/ rgyal bu 'jog rten dbang byug gi skye rabs/ rgyal po'i mdzad pa nyi shu ma gcig/ bka' chems ka bkam ma rnams mdo bskor/ 
5a6(mani bka' 'bum): // thugs rje chen po'i sgrub bskor gyi chos la/ sgrub thabs chen mo dang / sgrub thabs phran gnyis so// sgrub thabs chen mo'i bskor la/ drug bskor dang / sum bskor gnyis sa/ 
5a7(mani bka' 'bum): de gnyis la skyel lag dathubs dang / skos kyi bgad 'brel/ To ki dang / bskus dan rnams bshad chos yin no// sgrib thangs drug bskor ca ba las tshags dang bcas pa/ sum bskor rtsa ba/ gcig paskor te/ sa/ 
5b1(mani bka' 'bum): ni lag len sgrub chos so// sgrub thabs phran la/ sgrub thabs bsdus pa dang / 'bring po dang / rgyas pa thugs rje chen po'i gcig sgrub dang / gsum ni lag len gyi chos bskor yin no// rgyal ba gsum dril dang / 'jig
5b2(mani bka' 'bum): rten dbang phyug gnyis sku gsung thugs kyi sgrub thabs yin no// rta ma grin dregs pa dbang bsdud ni khro bos bgegs dbang du bsdud pa yin no// mkha' 'gro ma'i gsang bskor dang / gsang ba ye shes mkha'
5b3(mani bka' 'bum): 'gro dang / yi dam lnga dbang du bsdud pa gsum ni dbang bskud kyi chos gsum yin no// byin brlabs sba chos nad gdon sdig sgrib zhi bar byed pa byin brlabs nus pa'i bskor yin no// de rnams lag len gyi chos
5b4(mani bka' 'bum): sgrub bskor gyi phrin yin no// // zhal gdams kyi chos bskor la/ rgya tsho ba gzhan don du gdams pa dang / zab pa rang don du gdams pa gnyis su 'byed/ rgya che ba gzhan don gyi zhal gdams
5b5(mani bka' 'bum): la/ zhus lan gyi bskor la/ thugs rje chen po dngos la sprul pa'i rgyal pos zhus pa'i thugs rgyud dang / sprul pa'i rgyal po yab kyis zhus pa dang / yum gyis zhus pa dang / bal mo bza' khri btsun gyis zhus pa
5b6(mani bka' 'bum): dang / rgya mo bza' kong rngos zhus pa dang / sras gung bsrong gung btsan gyis zhus pa dang / sras mo khrom pa rgyan gyis zhus pa dang / phyi blon nang blon gyis zhus pa dang / zhal gdams brgyad po de zhus lan gyi
5b7(mani bka' 'bum): bskor yin no// yab la ngo sprod du gdams pa dang / yum la ngo sprod du gdams pa dang / bal mo bza' la nga sprod du gdams pa dang / rgya mo bza' la ngo sprod du gdams pa dang / sras la ngo sprid du gdams
6a1(mani bka' 'bum): pa dang / sras mo la sprod du gdams pa dang / rlung byon lnga ngo spyod du gdams pa dang / phyi blon ladu spyod du gdams pa dang / zhal gdams brgyad po deng snod du gdams pa'i bskor yin no// / rab sum/ 
6a2(mani bka' 'bum): la 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs su gdams pa dang / sras la rgyal srid ches kyis zung cig par bstan pa dang / lha gcig khrim brgyan la zhal thams su bstan pa dang / bal mo bza'i lathugs dam bka' rgyas btab pa dang / rgyu
6a3(mani bka' 'bum): mo bza' la gsang gtam gal cher gdams pa dang / nang blon la gdams pa dang / phyi blon la gdams pa dang / blon 'bangs rnams gdoms pa dang / bod 'bangs spyi la gdams pa dang / nang 'khor gyi bud med rnams la gdun
6a4(mani bka' 'bum): pa dang / phyi 'khor gyi bud med rnams la gdams pa dang / bud med spyi 'thun la gdams pa dang / bcu gnyis pa de zhal gdams bka' nan gyi bskor yin no// // yi ge drug pa la/ drug drug sum bcu rtsa drug/ yig
6a5(mani bka' 'bum): drug pa'i sngon tan gyi bzlas thabs drug/ wAzla'i spyod pa/ gtsol khor don brjod/ yige d+hag pa'i dgu phyugs bstod pa/ sku gsung thugs kyi bstod pa/ bkra shes smon lam dang brjid po de la gi drug pa'i gsung gi zhal gdas/ 
6a6(mani bka' 'bum): kyi bskor cig yin no// nyin nub lam khyer/ skyabs 'gro sems bskyed lam khyer/ rang de ni khyad par du 'phags pa'i lam khyer drug/ snang ba rin po che'i tshogs lam du 'khyer ba/ gtor ma lam khyer/ lnga po de lamakhye/ 
6a7(mani bka' 'bum): gyi zhal gdams kyi bskor yin no// / de rnams kyi bka' chos dang po'i shog dril gcig yin no// zhal gdams bskor gcig la/ drug tshan bcu pag gsum tshan bzhi bcu pa/ dpe don bzhi tshan bcu dgu pa/ drug tshan
6b1(mani bka' 'bum): kun drug pa/ bcu can d+hi DU na gsus pa/ lnga po zhal gdams thor bu'i bskor yin na/ dbang ba zla ba'i las rim sum bskor/ dbyung po 'bring gi las rim sum bskor/ dbang po rab kyi lam rim sum bskor
6b2(mani bka' 'bum): de gsum la ma rim sum bskor gyi zhal gdams yin na// 'khor ba 'jug bcug dang / bsgyu dgangs don rgyud gnyis mas 'jug las bzlog gi gal gdams so// de rnams ni bka' tshas par ma'i shog dri snye na/ 
6b3(mani bka' 'bum): rnal gdams bskor gcig la/ skye bo ma rig pa chos la 'dzud pa dang / chos po chos dang mi ldan pa chos la 'dzud pa dang / sngags pa sngags dang mi ldan pa sngags la 'dzud pa dang / rnal 'byor pa rnal 'byor pa dang / 
6b4(mani bka' 'bum): mi ldan pa rnal 'byor la 'jud pa dang / chos pa'i mtshang nas bskul ba dang / skye ba tha mal pa rnams kyi mtshang nas bskul ba dang / drug pa de 'tshang gi tshes drug gi zhal gdams so// / sgrub pa sgrub 'jug
6b5(mani bka' 'bum): drug chen sum bcun drug/ spyan can skyon med nyi shur+ya bAzhi/ des shes nyi shu rno bzhi/ dran pa nyi shA rtsa bzhi/ sgru pa de gang zag chos pa srung du gzhug pa'i zhal gdams// pa ra du phyin pa 'i ts+tsha/ bslab pa
6b6(mani bka' 'bum): drug sgrub pa'i mtha' drug/ bshod thabaso drug/ bzhi po de phyi nang gi chos bzhi'i zhal gdams yin// mtshan gyi zhal gdams// rig drug sku drug tu rang grol bar bstan pa/ khyad par du 'phags pa'i chos gdum
6b7(mani bka' 'bum): ying gisang khyad par 'phags pa'i chos gsum/ bzhi po de thugs rje chen po'i khyad par gyi zhal gdams yin// bar de drug gi gdames dang / 'pho bi bzhi'i gdams pa ni/ 'tsho ba'i rim pa la bslab pa dang / 'chi'i
7a1(mani bka' 'bum): mal dgos pa'i zhal gdam so// thun mong gi zhal gdams sum bcu rtsa drug pa/ ngo spyod khyad par can thun mong ma yin pa/ khyad par gyi zhal gdams drug gsum pa gsum thun mong khyad par gyi bslab pa'i zhal ga
7a2(mani bka' 'bum): yino// dam tshig gi gdams pa dang / skyabs 'gro'i gdams pa dang / sdom pa'i dmas pa dang / dbang dang byin brlabs kyi gdams pa dang / bzhi po de phyi nang gi bslab bya bzhi'i zhal gdam so// // skyabs 'gro sems bskyed bsngo
7a3(mani bka' 'bum): ba bsdus pa dang bcas pa/ gson gshin gyi bsngo ba yon bshad dang bcas pa/ bsnyen gnas bsrung mtshams dang bcas pa/ sems bskyed rgyas pa cho ga dang bcas pa/ dam tshig blang thabs sgrub lung dang bcas po/ bsnyen
7a4(mani bka' 'bum): sgrub kyi khog pa chen mo// dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dbang rim pa drug tu bskur ba/ tshig dbang rin po che dbang bzhi dang bcas pa/ cho ga'i rim pa brgyad po de gzhan la phan gdags shing rang smin pa'i zhal gdamaso// chos chen
7a5(mani bka' 'bum): de rnams ni bka' ches tha ma'i shog dril gcig/ shog dril gsum po de zhal gdams che tsho'i bskor yino// // zhal gdams zab don chung tsho'i bskor la/ yab kyis zhus pa la zab par gdams pa dang / yum gyis
7a6(mani bka' 'bum): zhus pa la zab par gdams pa dang / jo mo bal mo bzas zhus pa lnga gdams pa dang / jo mo rgya mo keng rngos zhus pa la zab par gdams pa dang / jo mo zhang zhung bza' li thig sman gyis zhus pa la zab par gdams pa dang

4a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): ming yang med/ pad+ma'i steng nga rdzas te skyes pa las/ skye ba rnam bzhi'i ming yang med/ g.yung drang tshel mnga' brnyes pa las// 
4b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): rgas shing rgud pa'i ming yang med/ skye shi med pa'i lam bsgoms pas/ skyes shing shi ba'i ming yang med/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing khams de na thams cad byang chub/ 
4b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): kyi lam la spyod pa las/ mi bde gnod pa'i ming yang med/ bde ba'i byang chub sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na// // stong pa nyid kyi gzhal med khang // rgyu
4b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): dang mtha' ni dpag tu med// phyi nang med pa chos kyi dbyings// mngon shes drug gi skar khung gsal/ mI mkhyen mi gzigs ci yang med// theg pa
4b4(mani bka' 'bum 2): chen po'i chos kyi gdugs phub pa/ byang chub yan log gi 'phan dang 'phyar ba// bdad pa ni 'joms pa'i rgyal mtshan snang ba/ mnyam pa nyid kyi
5a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): dkyil 'khor byas pa// chags pa med pa'i pad+ma bkram pa// rnam dag tshul khrims spos kyang 'thul/ sus kyang ma byas lhun gyis grub// ting 'ja
5a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): mi g.yo rgya mtsho las// rnam shes ma chags pad 'khrungs// chags med pad+ma'i 'od ldan las// tshad med bzhi'i gdan khri rtsigs// thugs rje snyoms pa'i
5a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): rgyan gyis brgyan// de na snang ba mtha' yas bzhigs// stobs bcu mi 'jigs sku yis brgyan// mtshan bzang dpe bad blta mi ngoms// 'od bzang sna
5a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): tshigs mnga' bzhin 'khor// zugs rje'i 'di bar daphyogs bcu 'phro// dpal kyi skyes bu mthu ldan pa/ skul bstobs chog mi shes/ 'khor ma
5b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): dag ni sprin ltar gtibs// mig ni mi g.yo mnyam pa zhag kyang // sngon gyi smon lam thugs rje yis// 'od zer mang po phyogs bcur 'phro// 'od zer re re'i rtse

6a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): mtha' yas 'od dpag tu med pa/ thugs rje che la thabs mkhas pa des/ 'gro ba'i don du thugs rjes gzigs nas/ lha pos

6a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): snang ba mtha' yas kyis snying rje chen pos 'gro den byed pa zhes bya bo'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas/ spyan g.yas pa las 'od
6a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): zi dkar po gcig las/ byang chub sems dpa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug tu sprul to// spyan g.yin pa las 'od zer sngon po gcig sa
6b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): lha mo sgrol mar sprul to// sprul pa de yang 'jig rton pa'i rgyal po la sogs pa/ dregs pa can 'dul ba'i phyir brdzus skyes pad+ma las sprul te/ mtsho pad+ma can zhes bya bar
6b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): 'od zer 'phros nas/ pad+ma las rdzus skyes su sku 'khrungs te/ de yang nub phyogs pad+ma can bde ba can gyi zhing khams na/ rgyal po rgyal rigs spyi bo nas dbang bskur/ 
6b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): ba 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po bzang mchog ces bya ba/ gling po no la mnga' mdzad pa/ longs spyod dang mnga' thad du 'dzem po gcig yod pa lus/ btsun mi
6b4(mani bka' 'bum 2): stong yod kyang sras rgyal ba med nas/ ci mdzad thams cad chos kyi longs spyod du mdzad pa las/ yul de na mtsho pad+ma can zhes bya ba gcig yod te/ mtsho de la me tog pad+ma
6b5(mani bka' 'bum 2): skye bas/ rgyal po dkon mchog la mchod pa byed pa'i tshe me tog len pa'i rkang mgyogs pa gtong bA las me tog blangs shing rgyal po la 'bul/ rgyal pos dkon

7a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): mA phub tsam de'i dbus na me tog gi snying po kha ma bye ba gsus pa tsam gcig 'dug nas ngo mtshar che ste/ rgyal po'i snyan du lo rgyus brjod pas/ rgyal po'i
7a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): zhal nas de'i nang na rdzus skyes sprul pa'i sku gcig bzhugs nges pa yin/ spyan drangs la mchod gnas byed dgos gsung nas dus de nyid du btsun mo dang / blon po dang
7a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): phyi 'khor dang / nang 'khor mang pos/ rgyal po'i spyan snga 'khod nas/ mtshol gzings bcus/ shing rta dang / mchod pa'i bye brag gdugs/ rgyal mtshan/ ba dan/ bla re/ rol
7a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): mo'i sgra mad+ma po dang / a ka ru dang / du ru ka la srogs pa'i bdug spos sna tshogs dang / kra shi ka'i ras gos mang po khyer nAs/ mtsho pad+ma can du phyin to// de nas mtsho la gzings

7b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): zhal nas sems can thams cad srong re rje zhes pa'i sgra bzlogs pa cag byon par gyur to// do nas rgyal po 'khor dang bcas pas phyag btsal// rgyal bas ka sha ka' ras kyi slob mos spyan drangs nas/ shang rdul phyobs sngar rgyu
7b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): mchod pa thams cad kyis mchod nas/ rgyal ba'i pho brang du spyan drangs te mchod granas mdzad cing bzhugs so// khye'u de'i mtshan yang pad+ma las skyes pas rje rnalas byes bya pad+ma'i snying po zhes kyang bya'o// de nas chos skyong
7b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): ba'i rgyal po des rang gi ston pa sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas la/ sprul pa 'di gang gi sprul pa lags/ 'di'i ming tsa yin zhes gsol pas/ sangs rgyas snang ba mthi' ba mtha' yas kyi zhal nas/ rgyal po chen

8a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): ni brag ltar gtams/ phra dog na rlung ltar g.yongs nas/ bdag dang bdag gar 'dzin pa'i lcags sgrog dam pas bsdams te/ 'khor ba'o sdug bsngal mo 'obs dang 'dra ba na snying rdzobar gzigs
8a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): nas/ spyan cha bshor ro// de la spyan tsha ba g.yas pa las lha mo sgrol ma dang / spyan chab g.yon pa las lha mo gnyer can byon no// sgrol ma'i zhal nas rigs kyi bu sems can gyi don byed pa la byang chub kyi sems
8a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): sbyongs shig gsung ngo // lha mo khro gnyer ma'i zhal nas rigs kyi bu sems can gyi don byed pa la thugs g.yel bar ma mdzad cig/ kho mo bcag gnyis kyis kyang rigs kyi bu khyod kyi grogs bya'o gsung nas

8b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / oM ma Ni pad me hUM/ de nas sprul pa'i sku thugs rje chen po 'phags pa spyan gzigs dbang phyug des sems can na mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i don mdzadado//

8b6(mani bka' 'bum 2): rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis 'gro ba'i don mdzad par dbang bskur/ sku las 'od zer bsam gyis mi khyab dpag gis mi lang ba cig 'phros nas longs spyod rdzogs sku'i zhing khams

9a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): der sprul skra'i sangs rgyas mang po sprul/ sprul pa'i sku de rnams kyi thugs kha nas kyang 'od zer brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'phros/ de las 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyag dang / khro gnyer
9a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): ma dang / sgrol ma yang sems can gyi grangs dang mnyam par sprul nas 'gro ba sems can gyi don mdzad do// yang sku las 'od zer spros te/ rgyu bkod pa bar ma'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rdul phra rab ji snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi/

9b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): rgyas kyi mdzad pa dang rnam par 'phral pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa gang la gang 'dul du sprul nas/ sems can gcig kyang ma lus pa bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bgod par bya'o// de la ma bkod par rang zhi bde/

9b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): kyi bu bdag la sogs pa phyogs bcu dus gsum na bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang tshul de lta bu dang / smon lam de lta bu la brten nas sangs rgyas pa yin pas/ khyod sems can gyi don byed pa'i grogs ngas

9b5(mani bka' 'bum 2): byas nasalha 'dul ba'i don du lha'i thub pa brgya byin du gyur la/ dga' bde 'dod chags kyi dbang gis lha ltung ba'i sdug bsngal ya re nga na/ gal te bdag lha'i gnas su phyin par gyur na/ 'chi 'pho lhung ba'i sdug bsngal zhi ba
9b6(mani bka' 'bum 2): gyur cig/ ces bya ba'i chos kyi sgra byung ngo // 'od zer la la lha ma yin gyi gnas su 'phros nas/ lha ma yin 'dul ba'i don du lha ma yin gyi thub pa thag bzangs ris su gyur la/ nga rgyal khong khro'i dbang gis 'thab rtsod kyi sdug bsngal
9b7(mani bka' 'bum 2): ya reng na/ gal te bdag lha ma yin gyi gnas su phyin par gyur na/ 'thab rtsod 'chi 'pho'i sdug bsngal zhi bar gyur cig/ ces bya ba'i chos kyi sgra byung ngo // 'od zer la la mi'i gnas su khyab par byas nas/ mi 'dul ba'i don du
10a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): ba'i don du// mi'i thub pa shAkya thub par gyur la/ 'dod sred chags pa'i dbang gis las btsan nas/ skye rga na 'chi'i sdug bsngal ya re nga na/ gal te bdag mi'i gnas su phyin par gyur na// mi 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal/

10a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): yi dgas 'dul ba'i don du/ yi dgas kyi thub pa na mkha' mdzod du gyur la/ ser sna las kyi dbang btsan nas/ bkres skom gyi sdug bsngal ya re nga na/ gal te bdag yo dgas kyi gnas su phyin par gyur na/ bkres skom nyam
10a5(mani bka' 'bum 2): thag zhi nas bde ba thob par gyur cig/ ces bya ba'i chos kyi sgra byung ngo // 'od zer la la dmyal ba'i gnas su 'phros te/ dmyal ba 'dul ba'i don du/ dmyal ba'i thub pa chos kyi rgyal por gyur la/ zhe sdang las kyi dbang btsan
10a6(mani bka' 'bum 2): nas/ tshal grang bsad bcad kyi sdug bsngal ya reng na/ gal te bdag dmyal ba'i gnas su phyin par gyur na/ dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal tsha grang bsang bcad mnar med kyi sdug bsngal zhi bar gyur cig/ ces bya ba'i chos kyi
10a7(mani bka' 'bum 2): sgra byung ngo // de ltar 'gro drug sdug bsngal las thar pa'i glags med pas/ lcags kyi za ma tog kha bcad pa dang 'dra bar gnas pa las 'od zer de la sbrul sku thub pa drag shar/ chos kyi sgra de thos pas 'gro ba rigs drug
10b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): gi sems can thams cad spongs par bton pa dang / thugs rje chen pos ri rab kyi cher byin te ye shes kyi spyan gyis gzigs pas/ yang snga ma de tsam du 'dug nas/ yan gsum du thabs dang snying rjes bton pas kyang sems can/ 
10b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): gyi khams la skye 'gri mi 'dug nas thugs mug/ yi chad nas kye ma bde bar gshegs pa'i dgongs pas 'dul ba'i zhing khams bsam gyis mkhyab/ namakha'i khams bsam gyis mi khyab/ sems can gyi khams bsam gyis
10b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): mi khyab pa bden par 'dug/ ngas de tsam pa'i sems can gton yang nyung ngu ma song bas 'khor ba 'di mi stongs par 'dug/ sems can gyi don mi 'grub par 'dug/ rang zhi bde thob par byas nas mya ngan las 'das pas/ 
10b4(mani bka' 'bum 2): rgyas kyi sa la gnas par bya'o// snyam pa dang / sngar gyi sems bskyed dam bca' nyams nas/ dbu tshal pa bcu rags so// de nas na tsham bzod nas/ skad ngan phyung ste/ kye ma ho/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thugs rje
10b5(mani bka' 'bum 2): dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas 'od dpag tu med pa bdag rang gi don ni ma bgyis sems can gyi don byas pas ma grub pas sdug bsngal lo// kyi hud kyi hud ces bshums pas/ sangs rgyas 'od dpag med kyis/ thugs rje chen
10b6(mani bka' 'bum 2): po'i dbu 'ubs bsdus nas zhal bcu gcig tu byin gyis brlabs so// zhi bas mi thul ba la khro zhal nag por byin gyis brlabs so// 'khor ba la thog ma dang tha ma med pa sems can gyi don 'khor ba ma stongs kyi bar du gyis
10b7(mani bka' 'bum 2): shig ces gsungs pa dang / 'phags pa spyan ros gzigs kyis 'di skad ces sbas so// bdag gis sems can gyi don 'khor ba ma stongs kyi bar du byed na/ bdag lag pa stong mig stong dang ldan par gyur la/ lag pa spring
11a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po stong du gyur/ mig stong bskal bzang po'i sangs rgyas stong du gyur nas/ gang la gang 'dul gyis 'gro ba'i don byed par gyur cig ces brjod pa dang / skad cig de nyid la/ phyag stong gi mthil na/ 
11a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): spyan stong yod pa'i zhal bcu gcig par gyur to// de nas sangs rgyas sdang ba mtha' yas kyis bka' stsal pa/ thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa'i 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug/ 'gro ba rigs drug tu skye ba'i sems can
11a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): rnams kyi skye ba'i sgo gcod pa'i yi ge drug pa 'dis/ 'gro drug gi skye sgo gcod pa yin no// oM maNi pad me hU~M/ zhes pa 'dis/ oM gyis lha'i skye sgo gcod/ mas lha ma yin gyi skye sgo gcod/ cis mi'i skyes sgo gcod/ pad kyis byol/ 
11a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): song gi skye sgo gcod// mes yi dgas kyi skye sgo gcod/ hU~M gis dmyal ba'i skye sgo bcad nas// 'gro ba rigs drug gi gnas stongs par byed pa yin pas 'di zung shig/ tshangs shig lhogs shig/ kun chub par gyis shig/ ces bka'
11a5(mani bka' 'bum 2): stsal to// 'phags pa spyan gzigs dbang phyug gis/ dang po byang chub kyi mchog tu sems bskyed nas 'gro ba rigs drug thabs kyis btul bas/ 'khor ba ma stongs nas// sems bskyed nyams pa dang / slar sems bskyed

11b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): snying po me tog gis brgyan pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams mang po sprul te/ de ni che ba'i rgyar mi 'jed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'bum phrag bcu'i rdul phra rab dang mnyam mo// de'i steng na sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad gangs
11b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): chen mtsho de dang mnyam pa cig bzhugs so// de'i ba spu'i khong bu thams cad khams mi 'dra bas bkang nas sems can gyi don mdzad do// yang ba spu'i bu ga gyen du bstan pa thams cad 'jig rten gyi khams gzhi mnyam pa zhes
11b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): bya ste/ sangs rgyas byon nas sems can gyi don mdzad do// yan man lhas pas rgya theb rtsegs pa 'dra'o// ba spu'i bu ga 'phreng la ltas pa rnams kyi ming nges phyal pa zhes bya ste/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas byon nas sems can gyi
11b4(mani bka' 'bum 2): don mdzad do// phan tshun ltas pas ni za 'og gur khang 'dra'o// ba sru'i bu ga 'thur la bstan pa la ni gan log gi 'jig rten gyi khams zhes bya ste/ sems can rang rang dang mnyam par sprul nas sems can gyi don mdzad do// 
11b5(mani bka' 'bum 2): rnam par snang mdzad de'i phyag mnyam bzhag gi stong na spos kyi rgya mtsho chen po yod pa'i nang nas/ pad+ma'i sdong po chen po cig skyes pa las ze 'bru dpag tu med pa yod do// de re re la yang zhing khams dpag tu med pa yod/ ze 'bru'i
11b6(mani bka' 'bum 2): dbus na zhing khams nyi shu rtsa lnga rtsegs yod/ bcu gsum pa mi 'jed 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas shakya thub pas 'dul ba'i zhing khams 'di yin/ 'dir skyes pa'i sems can rnams yid shas che ste/ 'jig rten gyi kha/ 
11b7(mani bka' 'bum 2): gzhan du dge sdig bskal bar spyad pa bas/ 'dir dge sdig cas byas pa nus pa che'o// de ltar 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i zhing khams su sku lus kyi bkod pa bsam gyis
12a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): gyis mi khyab pa sprul nas/ sems can gyi don mdzad do// longs spyod rdzogs pa'i skus 'dul ba'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// / oM ma Ni pad+ma me hUM/ yang byang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa spyan ras
12a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): gzigs dbang phyug des/ sbrul skus 'dul ba'i zhing khams la/ dang po zhing khams 'chags lugs ni/ pad+ma'i ze 'bru stong pa nas rlung langs nas/ rlung gi dkyil 'khor zla ga me chen po che sred med kyi bu'i stobs kyis kyong mi
12a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): mi shigs pa chags/ de'i steng du sprin chu'i snying po can gyi sprin 'dus pa las char gnya' shing gi rgyun tsam babs pas/ chu'i dkyil 'khor zlum po dkar po cig chags/ de rlung gis srubs pa las/ chu gser gyi snying po can
12a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): las/ rtagaser gyi sa gzhi gru bzhir chags/ de'i steng du khams sna tshogs kyi sprin chags/ char glang po che'i pho mtshan tsam babs pa las phyi'i rgyu mtsho tshugs/ de srid pa'i rlung gis bsru bas ri bo mchog rab/ gser gyi ri/ 
12a5(mani bka' 'bum 2): bdun rta bar gyi rol mtsho bdun// gling bzhi/ gling phran bcu gnyis/ phyi'i lcags ri dang bcas pa chags/ de ltar phyi snod kyi 'jig rten mos kyi chags/ nang bcud kyi sems can 'dod lha rigs drug dang / gzugs khams

12a7(mani bka' 'bum 2): thugs kha nas 'od zer bye ba phrag brgya bkye ste/ 'dzam bu'i gleng bye ba phrag brgya stsal/ 'jam bu'i gling re re'i dbus na rdo rje gdan re ri so pa'i sbub mar song / dbang chen gser gyis gzhi la thug/ sku bzhu nas 'dril na/ 
12b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): byang chub kyi shing skyes/ 'od zer re re la dga' ldan gyi lha gnas re re chags/ der lha'i bu de ba tog bkar po re re sprul/ sangs rgyas stong rdo rje gdan gcig pa la sangs rgya ba yin no// sangs rgyas stong rtsa gnyis kyang byang chub sems da/ 
12b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): dpa' rnams kyi mchog 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi rnam 'phrul yin no// de yang phyag stong las 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po skyong dang / spyan stong las bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas stong du sprul nas 'gro ba'i don sa/ 
12b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): pa las/ sngon sangs rgyas mar me mdzad chen po'i bstan pa la/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po yul 'khor bsrung zhes bya ba/ gling bzhi la mnga' mdzad pa cig la/ btsun mo stong rtsa gnyis yod/ btsun mo stong la sras stong yod pa
12b4(mani bka' 'bum 2): las/ btsun mo de rnams kyi nang nas khyad par du 'phags pa dpe med ma bya ba dang / ma smad ma bya ba gnyis yod pa las sras med pas/ btsun mo gnyis kyis khrus byas rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan nas/ dkon mchog la gsol ba bta
12b5(mani bka' 'bum 2): de'i nyin par rgyal po dang / btsun mo 'khor dang bcas pas tsan dan nags tshal pad+ma'i gling du skyo bsang la byon pa dang / btsun mo gnyis kyi lag tu me tog re re byon nas/ de gnyis kyi kha phye nas lhas pas khye'u gzugs mdzes/ 
12b6(mani bka' 'bum 2): pa re re byung ste/ dpe med ma'i khye'u de la chos kyi sems dpa' bya bar btags/ ma spyad ma'i khye'u de la chos kyi blo gros bya bar btags so// chos skyong ba'i rgyal po des sras de rnams sangs rgya bar shes nas/ gling bzhi'i
12b7(mani bka' 'bum 2): rab dang bcas pa rin po che sna tshogs las byas pa'i maN+Dal bshams/ mchod pa rgya chen po byas/ sras thams cad kyi ming bris/ rin po che sna tshogs kyis rgyan pa'i phra men gyi bum par bcug nas/ zhag bdun du mchod pa dang khrus
13a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): byas/ bum pa'i nang nas ming tsho bton pas/ thog mar 'khor ba 'jig byung / de'i bstan pa 'di tsam du gnas par gyur cig byas nas smon lam btab po// de'i rjes su gser thub byung / de'i rting la 'od bsrang byung / 
13a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): de'i rting la maur me mdzad byung / de'i rting la shAkya thub pa byung / de'i rting la byams pa la sngags pa rims kyis byung / kun gyi mthar mos pa byung ngo // de rnams kyis bstan pa 'di tsam du gnas par shog shig byas nas smon lam
13a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): btab po// de nas bcud mos pa la gong gi phu bo rnams kyis sems can gyi don byed pa la nged cag rnams kyis chog/ khyod rang sems can gyi don bya bka' bas zhi ba de la sdod cig ces smras pa dang / bcung mos pas smras pa
13a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): sems can gyi khams la zad pa med pas/ khyed cag rnams log pa'i bstan pa tsam zhig bdag gi bstan pa la gnas par shog shig ces smon lam btab po// chos kyi sems dpas khyed rnams sangs rgyas pa'i tshe bstan/ 
13a5(mani bka' 'bum 2): pa la gnod pa bsrung bar shog shig ces smon lam btab po// de ni dpal phyag na rdo rje yin te/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa bsrung ba'o// chos kyi blo gros kyis khyed rnams sangs rgyas pa'i tshe/ chos kyi
13a6(mani bka' 'bum 2): bskul ma 'debs par shog shig ces smon lam btab po// de ni lha tshangs pa dbu gsum pa yin te/ de na sangs rgyas stong po thams cad la chos gsung bar bskul ma 'debs pas kyang gang gis kyang
13a7(mani bka' 'bum 2): domi zlogs pa yin no// de ltar bskal pa bzang po 'di la sangs rgyas stong rdo rje gdan gcig la sangs rgyas pa yin no// sangs rgyas stong dang sems dpa' gnyis byung ba'i le'u ste drug pa'o// 
13b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): oM ma Ni pad me hUM/ de nas sngon tshe lo brgyad khri thub pa'i dus na/ sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig bya ba'i bstan pa byung ste/ sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig ces bya ba des/ rang sems/ 
13b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): sangs rgyas su rang gis rtogs nas sangs rgyas pas/ ming yang 'khor ba 'jig ces bya'o// sangs rgyas de la bram ze'i khye'u dub pa med pa zhes bya bas sems bskyed pa dang / sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig gis lung
13b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): bstan pa/ bram ze'i khye'u khyod tshe lo bzhi khri'i dus su/ zhing khams chos kyi mchod srang zhes bya bar sangs rgyas gser thub ces bya bar sangs rgya bar 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan nas sangs rgyas so// sangs rgyas

13b5(mani bka' 'bum 2): rgyas 'od bsrung gis lung bstan pa/ bram ze'i khye'u khyod tshe lo khri'i dus su zhing khams skar ma'i 'od ces bya bar/ sangs rgyas mar me mdzad ces bya bar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgya bar 'gyur ro zhes
13b6(mani bka' 'bum 2): lung bstan nas sangs rgyas so// sangs rgyas mar me mdzad la bram ze'i khye'u kai ru zhes bya bas/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / sangs rgyas mar me mdzad kyi lung bstan pa/ bram ze'i khye'u khyod 'jig rten gyi khams
13b7(mani bka' 'bum 2): mi mjed ces bya bar tshe lo brgya pa'i dus su/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa zhes bya bar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgya bar 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan to// snga rabs 'das pa'i sangs rgyas lung bstan pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// 
14a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): oM ma Ni pad ma hU~M/ de nas sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa sprul pa'i skus 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa ni/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis mthar phyung ste/ dang po 'jig rten pa'i mdzad pa lnga la/ dang po kho na dga' lnga/ 
14a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): gyi gnas nas 'pho ba ni/ bram ze'i khye'u ke'u bya ba de tshe 'phos pa dang / dga' ldan gyi gnas su lha'i bu dam pa tog dkar po zhes bya ba skye ba gcig gis thogs pa'i byang chub sems dpar sprul/ lha rnams la dgung lo dgur chos kyi 'a
14a3(mani bka' 'bum 2): lo bskor// de nas rang gi lung bstan pa rjes su dran pas/ gling bzhi'i mi rnams 'dul bar gzigs te/ 'phags pa byams pa la rgyal chab bskos te/ dga' ldan gyi gnas nas lho 'dzam bu gling du gshegs pa la gzigs thabs rnam/ 
14a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): pa bzhi las/ gling lho'i 'dzam bu gling la gzigs/ rigs rgyal po shAkya'i rigs la gzigs/ yul rgya gar bai rA na se grong khyer ser skya la gzigs/ dus bskal pa bzang po che lo brgya pa la gzigs nas/ lho 'dzam bu'i gling
14a5(mani bka' 'bum 2): gi mi rnams chos kyis 'dul bar dgongs te gshegs/ de yang ji ltar gshegs na/ glang po che mche ba drag pa dngul gyi mdog 'dra ba/ mgo me shel lta bu mdog dmar ba lus gser gyi dra bas g.yogs pa cig tu sprul nas/ sprin
14a6(mani bka' 'bum 2): gyi bseb par snang na phar rdo rje'i 'gros kyis bzhud do// de ni mdzad pa dang po dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba'o// de nas gnyis pa lhums su zhugs pa bstan pa ni yab rgyal po zas gtsang dang yum sgyu ma lha mdzes sras kyis pha
14a7(mani bka' 'bum 2): par gzigs nas glang gi lo dpyid zla ra ba nya'i dub so// yum sgyu ma lho mo mdzes grong khyer ser skya'i rgyal po'i khab kyi pho brang na/ gser gyi khri la gzims nas rnal ba las/ snyan khung g.yas pa na mar la gser gyi skas la ban+d+ha/ 
14b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): lhums su zhugs te/ yum gyi rmi lam du yang de ltar byung zhing lus kyang shin du bde bar gyur to// de'i dus su dpal lha las babs pa'i mchod rten byung ngo // de nas mdzad pa gsum pa yum gyi lhums nas bltams pa ni/ 
14b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): zlo ba bcu nas yum sku bsrel snam bgyid nas/ ldum pa'i tshal du byon nas shing grag shul sku brten te/ g.yog mo skye rgu'i bdag mos sku brten nas/ yum gyi mchan khung g.yas pa nas nu cha med par bde ba dang ldan pas sku ba/ 
14b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): te/ lnga tshangs pas dar dkar gyi sleb mos blangs/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis bdud rtsi'i chu'i sku khrus gsol// phyogs bzhir gom pa bdun bdun bor bas/ pad+ma bdun bdun byung ste de'i dus su pad+ma brtsegs pa'i mchod
14b4(mani bka' 'bum 2): chen byung ngo // de nas mdzad pa bzhi pa rgyal bu rol rtsed mdzad pa rig pa'i gnas sde la mkhas pa ni/ ma ma sum bcu rtsa lnga la gtad te/ khrus byed pa'i mam bdun/ nu ma skyed pa'i mam bdun/ rkyen 'dogs pa'i ma ma bdun phyas/ 
14b5(mani bka' 'bum 2): drar byeng ba'i mam bdun/ cid me byed pa'i mam bdun/ ma ma de rnams la gtad do// de nas lo bcur yig dang / ces dang sran dang / bzo dang / sgra dang / reg pa'i gnas sde la bslabs pas/ bslab ma dgos par rang 'khrungs
14b6(mani bka' 'bum 2): shes nas/ slob dpon rnams kyi mi shes pa yang rgyal bus shes pas/ mtshan rgyal bu don thams cad grub par btags so// rgyal bu byang chub kyi zhing gi bsil grib la bzhugs pa la/ bu sring ma rnams kyis gser dngul dang mu tig

15a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): kha ba bzhes par zhus pas ma gnang nas/ yab kyis yang dang yang du zhus pas/ bzhug tu bud med yon tan sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang ldan pa cig rnyed na blang bar zhal gyis bzhes pas/ de shAkya lag na be con gyi bu mo shakya sa/ 
15a2(mani bka' 'bum 2): 'tsho ma la tshang nas blangs pas/ lha sbyin na reng kha snga zer nas ma 'cham pa la/ sa 'tsho ma'i yab kyis sgyu rtsal gang tshe la ster zer nas/ lo bcur bdud dang sgyu rtsal 'gran te/ chu rtsal dang / sred dang / stobs dang / mda' 'phong dang / yi ge

15b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): ba ni/ de nas chu bo na ra dza ra'i 'gram du dka' thub la gshegs pa la/ tshong dpon gyi bu bkra shis kyi sardza ku sha phul ba de blangs te/ dka' thub lo drug mdzad pas lus kyang shin du rid par gyur to// de nas ting nge 'dzin de las ba
15b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): nas gshegs pas/ bram ze'i bu mo legs skyes ma tshogs sog pa gzigs nas/ bsod snyoms la byon pa dang ba ser skya lnga brgya'i 'o ma gcig la gcig blud nas/ tha ma de'i 'o ma'i 'byams phul bas/ rgyal bu skags

15b4(mani bka' 'bum 2): nas phul d+ha byang chub sems dpas phyi dro yang rung chu btab nas gsol bas/ spre'u dga' nas gar byas pas khron pa'i nang du lhung nas tshe'i dus byas te sum bcu rtsa gsum po'i gnas su lha'i bu dri ma med par grags pa bya bar

17a4(mani bka' 'bum 2): 'dod khams kyi lnga bdud rag khro bya dang / r-ig ta bya ba gnyis kyis dpon byas nas/ bdud bye ba khrag khrig gis rnamakha' nas gzugs mi sdug pa sde tshugs bskrun nas/ mtshan tshwa sna tshogs char du phab/ bdud lha sbyin gyi/ 
17a5(mani bka' 'bum 2): dpag can gyi mdang 'ding bar byas pas/ mtshon na thams cad dz+ha ga car sna chags su rabs/ lci smyed myigacu rgyud kyang chung / byams pa chen po'i ting 'dzin gyis lha'i bu'i bdud bcom mo// sa sbyin gyi myangon / 
17a6(mani bka' 'bum 2): khang par zhugs pa dang / sring mo gzhon nu ma bzhis ming po ci nyes dris pas/ ngas go'u te ma ma thul byos pas/ gri'u ta ma nged kyis slu btub kyis zer nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i la lus kyi rgyun stan/ nu ma bstan ma
17a7(mani bka' 'bum 2): 'dod pa g.yo ba'i brda sbyar// ne co btang nis lus 'bul bya ba'i phrin btang bas/ byang chub sems dpos se gol berdebs pas rgan ma bzhir gyur/ lha sbyin gyis spras pa/ nged kyi mthul ba khyed kyis thul po ci yod/ 
17b1(mani bka' 'bum 2): gsol gyis zer/ yang lha sbyin na re go'u tam khyod kyis bskal pa stong du tshogs bsags zer ba brdzun/ dbang po su yin zer ba zhes smras pas/ byang chub sems dpa' phyag g.yas pa sa la brdabs nas/ nga'i dbang po/ 
17b2(mani bka' 'bum 2): 'di yin zhes byas pa dang / sa'i lha mo lte ba yan chad brten nas/ lag na bdud ci'i bum pa bzung ste tshogs bsogs pa'i dbang po nang yin no// zhes smras pa dang / lha sbyin ming sring gi bzod gsol byas gnas
17b3(mani bka' 'bum 2): dag sku lta mchog tu gzugs bzang ba// ye shes rgya mtsho ga ser gyi lhun po 'dra// grags pa 'jig rten gsum na ljang nge ba// mgon po mchog khyod la ni skyabs su 'chi// zhes brjod pas rgan mo pani sdung

26a1(mani bka' 'bum 2): mkhyen pa'i ye shes bshad par 'tshal bas/ bdag gis ji ltar thob par bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das bdag la yi ge drug pa bstsal ba de la/ 'dzam bu'i gling rin po che sna bdun gyis bkang ste dbul bar 'tshal lo//

6a1(mani bka' 'bum 3): gyes brlab pa ni/ rig pa gsal lam slebs pa mi 'gyur ba'i gdeng gis bdag gzhan byin gyis brlab pa'o// mtshon pa mnyam pa ris med byin gyis brlab pa ni/

6a3(mani bka' 'bum 3): na 'khor lo drug sgom/ nyamasu gang len na khyer so drug le ni/ bsdu na gang du bsdu na dgongs pa drug tu bsdu/ ngo gang du slong na bar ngo drug tu ngo sprod/ gnad gang du 'grol na bam
